select * where {$s $p $o}

------------------

PREFIX : <http://www.brightstardb.com/example/article#>
SELECT *
WHERE {
  $res a <http://www.brightstardb.com/example/article/> .
  $res :title $o .
}

------------------

PREFIX : <http://www.brightstardb.com/example/article#>
SELECT DISTINCT $res $title $abstr 
WHERE {
  $res a <http://www.brightstardb.com/example/article/> .
  $res :title $title .
  $res :abstr $abstr .
  $res :tags $any .
}
ORDER BY desc($res)
